 adaalat ne kaha ki un par mukadmaa raajnneeti se prabhavit or doshapurn he

 in jhadpon ke baad yamin ne kal apatkaal ghoshit kar diya

 nashid ne is halaat main bharat kii madad maangi

 tippaniyan The government refused to implement the order following which mass demonstrations began in the capital Male

 The drama 'apna Morcha' of 'sambhav' was very popular, in which Manoj acted
 actor ke liye anushaasan ko manoj bajpeyi jarur bataate hai
 He used to say that 'I have followed discipline in life
 abhinayta bananaa he to aapaki subah reharsal se shuru honi chahie, shikaayat se nahin
 This is your lifestyle, which makes you look different from any other person or actor '
 abhinayta ko prerana badalati rahani chahie
 So much of life cannot work with a single role model, so he said that my role models have been changing depending on the demand of acting '
 cinema yaa theatre ke liye diarector kii bhoomika ko ahm bataate hue unhone kaha ki mere liye kairectorigeshan kii-point rahaa he
 The director is supreme for me
 actor ko apane kaam se uske vijan ko ekstand karnaa chahie
 The actor is one who does not swallow the director '
 tippaniyan Stating the extent of cinema, Manoj Bajpayee also expressed his opinion on the debate on the censor board in the country
 unhone kaha ki 'sensor board bahut aloktantric he, hamaare jaise loktantr main
 Films should be rated according to the age group and the board should only give certificates
 abhibhavak behtareen sensor hote hai, agar wo kaam nahin karte to sensor bhi nahin kar sakegaa
 Sensors have lost their importance in this digital time '
 manoj bajepayi ne ek bahut jaruri baat kahi ki 'cinema or naatakon main ham realism shabd par bahut jor dete hai
 We are forgetting the character
 realism ke naam par desh main bahut bada frod chal rahaa he
 Significantly, during his struggle days, Manoj Bajpayee made several attempts for admission to NSD, but he failed

 enesdy main behtareen rangakarmiyon ke saath training hoti thi to abhinay kaa jo craft hota he, usko taraashne main madad milti'

 nirdeshak mere liye supreme he

 He said, "we have agreed to call a meeting of special representatives soon to find a fair, logical and acceptable solution to both sides of the border dispute
" " Manmohan said that although there have been differences between India and China, the relationship between the two countries has been redefined in the last 25 years
 manmohan ne kaha ki donon netaaon ne bharat-china seemaa ke pashchimi sector main ghati haal kii ghatana se siikhe sabak kaa jayja liya, or yah ki maujuuda seemaa tantra apane aap main kargar sabit hua
 Li said that China and India have worked to maintain peace and harmony in the border areas
 unhone kaha ki hamen seemaa tantra main sudhaar karne or use or prabhavi banane tathaa apane matbhedon ko sulajhane kii jarurat he
 Manmohan Singh also raised the issue of India's trade deficit
 saath hi tibet main brahmaputra nadi par baandh banane ke beijing ke nirnay par bhartiya chintaa se bhi lee ko avgat karaayaa

 It also sought to increase access to the Chinese market for Indian investors and exporters
 saath hi bharat kii aadharbhoot sanrachana evam vinirmaan ke kshetra main chini bhagidaari badhaane ke liye bhi aamantrit kiya
 india-china trade reached $ 66 billion in 2012
 jabaki 2000 main yah maatr teen arab dollar tha
 But the trade is tilted in favor of China
 varsh 2012 main vyapaar ghaataa 29 arab dollar ho gaya

 lee ne kaha, "hamaare bich mithravat, gambheer or spashtataa ke saath baatcheet hui
 The most important result of these discussions is that the leaders of the two countries have reached a strategic consensus and increased strategic trust between us
 " The two leaders discussed ways to connect India's Northeast with Bangladesh, Myanmar, China and other countries in South Asia
 tippaniyan Manmohan said that he hoped to visit China as soon as possible
 ek vishaal pratinidhimandal ke saath aae lee ab yahaan se mumbai jaaenge or vahaan se pakistan, switsraland or germany kii yatra par nikal jaaenge
 Lee arrived here on Sunday evening and had two rounds of talks with Manmohan Singh
 pehali baatcheet ravivaar ko ek nijee raatri bhoj par or duusari somvaar ko aupchaarik taur par
 Manmohan Singh has had the first meeting with a Chinese leader since his meeting with President Xi Jinping in Durban in March
 ullekhneey he ki chini sainik 15 april ko vaastavik niyantran rekha (elesi) ke paar bhartiya kshetra main 19 kilometre ghus aae the or vahaan unhone apane shivi laga rakhe the
 Tensions between the two countries increased after the incident surfaced
 yah vivaad paanch may ko tab samaapt hua, jab sainya or kootnithik str par kai daur kii chali baatcheet ke baad donon paksh 15 april se pehle kii sthiti behaal karne par sahamat ho gaye
 As expected, the issue arose during the talks between the two leaders
 manmohan ne lee ke saath samvaadadaataaon se kaha ki unke bich aapasi chintaa ke vibhinn muddon par vistrut va spasht charchaa hui
 The Prime Minister said that in a conversation with Li, he also recently raised the issue of Chinese Army incursions into Indian territory along the Line of Actual Control (LAC)
 lee ne bhi sur main sur milaate hue kaha ki bharat or china ranneetik saajhedaar or achche mitra hai
 Emphasizing the discussion on border dispute and river water dispute, he said that the two countries can talk with each other cleanly
 manmohan ne kaha ki bharat or china ke bich seemaa vivaad par baatcheet ke liye jald hi vishesh pratinidhiyon kii baithak hogi
 He said, "we have agreed to call a meeting of special representatives soon to find a fair, logical and acceptable solution to both sides of the border dispute
" " Manmohan said that although there have been differences between India and China, the relationship between the two countries has been redefined in the last 25 years
 manmohan ne kaha ki donon netaaon ne bharat-china seemaa ke pashchimi sector main ghati haal kii ghatana se siikhe sabak kaa jayja liya, or yah ki maujuuda seemaa tantra apane aap main kargar sabit hua
 Li said that China and India have worked to maintain peace and harmony in the border areas
 unhone kaha ki hamen seemaa tantra main sudhaar karne or use or prabhavi banane tathaa apane matbhedon ko sulajhane kii jarurat he
 Manmohan Singh also raised the issue of India's trade deficit
 saath hi tibet main brahmaputra nadi par baandh banane ke beijing ke nirnay par bhartiya chintaa se bhi lee ko avgat karaayaa
 The river flows from Tibet towards Arunachal Pradesh and Assam
 manmohan ne kaha ki unhone china ke pradhanmantri ke saath vyapaar ghate ko paatane par bhi charchaa kii
 It also sought to increase access to the Chinese market for Indian investors and exporters
 saath hi bharat kii aadharbhoot sanrachana evam vinirmaan ke kshetra main chini bhagidaari badhaane ke liye bhi aamantrit kiya
 india-china trade reached $ 66 billion in 2012
 jabaki 2000 main yah maatr teen arab dollar tha
 But the trade is tilted in favor of China
 varsh 2012 main vyapaar ghaataa 29 arab dollar ho gaya
 Lee said, "we had a friendly, serious and candid conversation
 in charchaaon kaa sabase mahatvapurn parinaam yah he ki donon deshon ke netaa ranneetik sahmati par pahunche hai or hamaare bich ranneetik vishwaas badha he
 " donon netaaon ne bharat ke purvottar ko bangladesh, myanmar, china or dakshin asia ke anya deshon se jodne ke tareekon par charchaa kii
 The comments manmohan ne kaha ki vah yathasambhav jald se jald china kaa daura karne kii aashaa rakhte hai
 Lee, who is accompanied by a large delegation, will now travel to Mumbai and from there travel to Pakistan, Switzerland and Germany

 Li also added that India and China are strategic partners and good friends
 seemaa vivaad or nadi jal vivaad par batcheet par bal dete hue unhone kaha ki donon desh safagoi ke saath aapas main baat kar sakate hai
 Manmohan said that special representatives will meet soon to discuss the border dispute between India and China
 unhone kaha, "hamane seemaa vivaad ke nishpaksh, taarkik evam donon pakshon ke liye sweekaarya samaadhaan nikaalane ke liye vishesh pratinidhiyon kii jald hi baithak bulaane par sahmati jataai he
 " manmohan ne kaha ki bharat or china ke bich haalanki matbhed rahe hai, lekin pichley 25 varsho main donon deshon ke sambandh nae sire se paribhaashit hue hai
 Manmohan said that the two leaders reviewed the lessons learned from the recent incident in the western sector of the india-china border , and that the existing border system proved to be effective in itself
 lee ne kaha ki china or bharat ne simavarti ilaakon main shanti evam sauhadrr banaae rakhane ke liye kaam kiya he
 He said that we need to improve and make the border system more effective and resolve our differences
 manmohan singh ne bharat ke vyapaar ghate kaa mudda bhi uthaaya
 Simultaneously apprised Li of Indian concern over Beijing's decision to build a dam on the Brahmaputra River in Tibet
 yah nadi tibet se arunachal pradesh or assam kii ore bahati he
 Manmohan said that he also discussed bridging the trade deficit with the Chinese Prime Minister
 saath hi bhartiya niveshkon evam niryaatkon ke liye chini bazaar main pahunch badhaane kii bhi maang kii
 Also invited to increase Chinese participation in the infrastructure and manufacturing sector of India
 bharat, china kaa vyapaar 2012 main 66 arab dollar pahunch gaya
 Whereas in 2000 it was just three billion dollars
 lekin vyapaar kaa palada china ke paksh main jhukaa hua he

 NDTV now has information about how that particular operation was carried out on 9 June
 21 special forces batalian ke commando jo ki purvottar ke ghaney jangalon kii ladaai main maahir hote hai, unhone dushmano kii harkaton par paini najar rakhi or apane nishane bahut saavdhaanee se chune
 On June 8, at 11 o'clock, these commandos entered deep forests and on foot entered the Myanmar border
 9 june kii subah 4:45 baje, suryoday se thodaa pehle hamale kaa vakt tha
 The incharge of the team that carried out this secret operation was a young lieutenant colonel (names cannot be given for security reasons)
 wo khud team kaa netritv kar rahaa tha
 Then there was a paratrooper whom he calls his friend, a sergeant and another paratrooper from his team
 in chaaron ko varshon tak purvottar ke ghaney jangalon main atyaadhik garmi or umas bhare maahaul main bhi ladane kii training mili he
 These four were the best for a military campaign that the Indian Army could have chosen - experienced and highly skilled in killing the country's enemies, and even entering the border of another country if needed
 aapako bataa den ki is oparation ke hafte bhar pehle hi aatankwaadiyon ne 18 javaanon ko maar daalaa tha
 The government was committed to proving its strong intentions to fight terrorism, even if it had to sneak into another country and conduct a secret campaign
 leftinent karnal ne do nishane tay kiye the
 Havildar and his paratrooper attacked the post at a short distance, while the team leader accompanied his friend to the other post
 is kshetra main chal rahe vidrohiyon ke training camp ke ek post par aatanki us vakt bhi sakriya the
 His people were cautious
 lekin jangal main chhupate hue hawaldaar apane paratrupar ke saath rengte hue us post tak pahunchaa
 The paratrooper visited the area while the sergeant crawled to the enemy post where a gun-toting terrorist was present
 post par tainaat aatankwaadi kii mashinagan jis suraakh se baahar nikali hui thi wo uski pahunch se zyada dur nahin thi
 The sergeant immediately set the terrorist's hideout with the gun with his silencer through the same hole
 uske baad usne ek anya aatanki ko sir main goli maari jabaki duusare ko behad kareeb se goli maari
 This entire action took less than a minute
 iske baad behad khamoshi se wo jhaadiyon main gum ho gaye or apane commanding officer, leftinent karnal ko teen aatankiyon ko maar giraane kii khabar di
 After that they started waiting and vahaan se thodi hi duuri par leftinent karnal or uskaa paratrupar dost bina koi aawaaj kiye duusare post par pahunch gaye
 He killed two terrorists with his silencer Uzi sub machine gun and immediately came out of the second post
 vahaan se kareeb 30 meter kii duuri par dushman kaa ek bunker tha
 Some sounds were coming from the bunker, the lieutenant colonel threw a grenade into the bunker and then went inside
 agar leftinent karnal ne sochaa tha ki ek grenade se saare aatanki maare jaaenge to wo galat tha
 Four terrorists were injured inside the bunker and they also tried to attack
 lekin leftinent karnal ne apni uji se chaaron ko maar giraaya
 The colonel then ordered a team of Indian para commandos waiting nearby to attack the terrorist camps vigorously
 uske nirdesh par special forces ke 21 commando ne rocket propeld grenade se apane nishane par 20 minute se bhi zyada vakt tak firing karte rahe
 The comments ab tak bhartiya commando ne jis camp par hamalaa kiya tha isaki jaankaree aatankiyon ko ho chuki thi or kareeb ilaake ke 10-12 banksron se bhartiya commando team par firing hone lagi
 But the Indian Army had broken its back with a rocket propelled grenade attack and the four commandos on the spot, who were taking on the terrorists, clashed with the terrorists running towards the Indian border
 is oparation ke liye shaury chakra vijeta yuva leftinent karnal ko kirti chakra pradaan kiya gaya jo ki shaantikaal kaa doosraa sabase bada bahaduri puraskaar he
 And the Havildar, who attacked the first post of the enemy, was awarded the Shaurya Chakra which is the third highest gallantry award given during the first peacetime

 is gupt oparation ko anjaam dene vaali team kaa incharge ek yuva leftinent karnal (suraksha kaarnon se naam nahin bataae ja sakate) tha
 He himself was leading the team
 uske baad tha ek paratrupar jise wo apana dost bataate hai, ek hawaldaar or usee kii team kaa ek anya paratrupar
 These four have been trained to fight in extreme heat and humid environment in the thick forests of the Northeast for years
 aise sainya abhiyaan ke liye ye chaaron sarvshereshth the jinako bhartiya sena chun sakati thi - desh ke dushmano ko maar giraane main anbhavi or behad nipun, or jarurat pade to duusare desh kii seemaa main ghus kar bhi
 Let us tell you that a week before this operation, 18 soldiers were killed by terrorists
 sarkaar aatankwaad se ladane ko lekar apane majboot iraade sabit karne ke liye patibaddh thi, bhale hi iske liye kisi duusare desh main ghuskar gopneey abhiyaan chalaanaa pade
 The lieutenant colonel had set two targets
 hawaldaar or uske paratrupar ne thodi hi duuri par sthit post par hamalaa kiya jabaki team leader ne apane dost ke saath duusare post par
 The terrorists were also active at a post of the rebels' training camp in the region at that time
 unke log satark the
 But while hiding in the forest, the sergeant crawled with his paratrooper and reached the post
 paratrupar ne ilaake kaa muyna kiya jabaki hawaldaar reng kar dushman kii us post par pahunch gaya jahaan ek bandookdhaari aatanki maujuud tha
 The hole from which the machine gun of the terrorist posted on the post was not far from his reach
 hawaldaar ne turant hi usee suraakh ke jariye apni silencer lagi bandook se aatanki ko thikaane laga diya
 He then shot another terrorist in the head, while the other shot very closely
 is puri karrwai main ek minute se bhi kam vakt laga
 After this, he went into the bushes with great silence and informed his commanding officer, Lieutenant Colonel, of killing three terrorists
 uske baad wo intjaar karne lage or a short distance from there, the lieutenant colonel and his paratrooper friend reached the second post without making any sound
 usne apni silencer lagi uji sab mashinagan se do aatankiyon ko maar giraaya or duusari post se turant hi baahar aa gaya
 There was a bunker of the enemy about 30 meters from there
 bunker se kuch awaajen aa rahi thim, leftinent karnal ne bunker main ek grenade phenkaa or phir andar chalaa gaya
 If the lieutenant colonel thought that all the terrorists would be killed by a grenade, it was wrong
 bunker ke andar 4 aatanki ghayal pade the or unhone hamalaa karne kii koshish bhi kii
 But the Lieutenant Colonel killed all four with his Uzi
 uske baad karnal ne paas hi intjaar kar rahe bhartiya para commando kii team ko aatanki campon par joardaar hamalaa karne ke aadesh die
 On his instructions, 21 commandos of the Special Forces kept firing on their targets with rocket propelled grenades for more than 20 minutes
 tippaniyan Till now the terrorists had come to know about the camp which was attacked by the Indian commandos and the Indian commando team started firing from 10-12 bunkers of the area
 lekin bhartiya sena ke rocket propeld grenade hamale se unki qamar tod di thi or maukey par maujuud chaaron commando jo aatankiyon se loha le rahe the, bhartiya seemaa kii ore bhaag rahe aatankiyon se bhid gaye
 The Kirti Chakra was awarded to the young lieutenant colonel, the winner of the Shaurya Chakra for this operation, which is the second highest gallantry award of the peacetime
 or dushman ke pehle post par hamalaa karne vaale hawaldaar ko shaury chakra pradaan kiya gaya jo ki pehle shaantikaal ke dauraan diya jane vaala teesraa sabase bada bahaduri puraskaar he
